trochaic verse
扬抑格诗
iambic meter
(诗的)抑扬格
iambic rhythm
抑扬格
An iambic foot consists of an unstressed syllable followed by a stressed syllable as in \'delay\'.
Yìyánggéshī zhōng de yīnbù shì yóu fēi zhòngdú yīnjié hòu gēnzhe yí gè zhòngdú yīnjié zǔchéng de，lìrú“delay\'。
抑扬格诗中的音步是由非重读音节后跟着一个重读音节组成的，例如“delay”。

xiē shǎnɡ
take a midday nap (or rest)
游了半天了，快上来歇会儿吧。
Yóu le bàntiān le，kuài shànglái xiē huìr ba。
You\'ve been swimming a long time now. Come out and have a rest.
从上午八点工作到下午两点一直没有停歇

歇一会儿
xiē yìhuìr
have a short rest

I\'m completely done in.

I\'ve been off from work for a week.
今天小王歇班。

Xiao Wang is off duty today.

He is not old but is already balding.

Jīntiān wǒmen zǎozao jiù xiēgōng le。
We stopped work early today.

xiē kǒu qìr
